### Post by Townley89 on 2012-01-01
Hi team,

I'm trying to install an ATI driver for my Radeon HD6850 card. I can install and activate the ATI/AMD Proprietary FGLRX graphics driver, but I'm unable to activate the post-release driver. This wouldn't be a problem but under the non-post-release, I can't save my settings (clicking apply simply closes the screen when I'm in the ATI Catalyst Center.) I'm using a dual monitor setup, and would like to extend my displays (not doable under the displays setting in the dash, as the width exceeds the virtual size.) 

When I try to install the post-release, I receive an error which says "Cannot install drivers. Check var/log/jockey.log. The contents of that file are included below, but I'm afraid I'm unable to make sense of the error and understand what it is that I must do to enable a proper install.

### Post by rsvancara on 2012-01-01
Can you run  dpkg -l |grep nvidia

I am guessing you still have nvidia drivers installed.  Just a guess.

---

### Post by Townley89 on 2012-01-01

robert@Battlecruiser:~$ dpkg -l |grep nvidia
